  <script>
   $(document).ready(function(){
			if( isBreakpoint('md') || isBreakpoint('lg') ) {
				$("[data-toggle='dropdown']").on("click", function(e){
					if((e.which == "1") && $(this).is(":hover") && !$(this).parents(".dropdown").hasClass("open")){
						e.stopImmediatePropagation();
						if ($(this).attr('target') !== "_blank" ) {
							document.location=$(this).attr("href");
						}
					}
				});
			}
			function isBreakpoint( alias ) {
				return $('.device-' + alias).is(':visible');
			}

			// makes href="tel:#"s valid for browsers
			$('a[href^="tel"]').each( function(){
				$(this).attr('href', 'tel:' + $(this).attr('href').replace(/\D+/g,""));
			});

			// prevents footer collapse animation on viewports when the
			// collapse element is already forced open
      $('footer [data-toggle="collapse"]').on('click', function(e){
        if ($('footer .collapse:not(.in)').is(':visible')) {
          e.preventDefault();
          e.stopPropagation();
        } else {
          return true;
        }
      });

			//Search-box code
			$('#search-box').submit(function() {
				var hr = 'default.asp?page=xAllInventory';
				var sqInit = $('#search-box .search_spacer').val();
				if (sqInit=='Search Here') sqInit=''; //change this to placeholder text
				var sq = sqInit.replace(/\./g, '');
				window.location.href = hr + (sq?'&sq='+sq:'');
				return false;
			});

		});
  </script>

    function trackEcommerce() {
    this._addTrans = addTrans;
    this._addItem = addItems;
    this._trackTrans = trackTrans;
    }
    function addTrans(orderID,store,total,tax,shipping,city,state,country) {
    ga('ecommerce:addTransaction', {
        'id': orderID,
        'affiliation': store,
        'revenue': total,
        'tax': tax,
        'shipping': shipping,
        'city': city,
        'state': state,
        'country': country
    });
    }
    function addItems(orderID,sku,product,variation,price,qty) {
    ga('ecommerce:addItem', {
        'id': orderID,
        'sku': sku,
        'name': product,
        'category': variation,
        'price': price,
        'quantity': qty
    });
    }
    function trackTrans() {
        ga('ecommerce:send');
    }
    var pageTracker = new trackEcommerce();

   $(document).ready(function(){
  $('.dropdown-submenu a.test').on("hover", function(e){
    $(this).next('ul').toggle();
    e.stopPropagation();
    e.preventDefault();
  });
});

$(function(){

	function is_touch_device() {
	  return !!('ontouchstart' in window);
	}

	if ( is_touch_device() ) {
		$('#main-nav .dropdown-toggle').attr('href','javascript:;');

		$('#main-nav .sub-dropdown-toggle').on('touchstart',function(e){
			e.preventDefault();
			e.stopImmediatePropagation();
			$(this).parent('li').toggleClass('open');
			$(this).siblings('.dropdown-menu').toggleClass('showSubMenu');
		});
	}

});

     <div>
      <h1>
       Welcome to Adventure Harley-Davidson®
      </h1>
      <h6>
       Dover, Ohio
      </h6>
      <div class="welcome-text">
       <a href="/about-us-harley-davidson-dealership--info">
        Adventure Harley-Davidson®
       </a>
       is an authorized
       <a href="/showroom/harley-davidson/family">
        Harley-Davidson®
       </a>
       dealership serving the Dover, Ohio area. We are proud to carry a large selection of
       <a href="/default.asp?page=xNewInventory">
        new
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/default.asp?page=xPreOwnedInventory">
        pre-owned
       </a>
       inventory. When you are ready to invest in a new
       <a href="/default.asp?page=xAllInventory">
        motorcycle
       </a>
       , our friendly and knowledgeable sales,
       <a href="/credit-financing-harley-davidson-dealership--financing">
        financing
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/service-repair-harley-davidson-dealership--service">
        service
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/parts-harley-davidson-dealership--parts">
        parts
       </a>
       departments are prepared to make sure your experience is outstanding, from assisting while you’re making your choice to ongoing maintenance and customization. At Adventure Harley-Davidson®, we value the opportunity to create a
       <a href="/reviews-testimonials-harley-davidson-dealership--xtestimonials">
        long term relationship
       </a>
       with our customers, and we do that by giving you the best customer service available.
       <br/>
       Call us at 330.364.6519 or
       <a href="/map-hours-directions-harley-davidson-dealership--hours">
        stop by
       </a>
       today and experience our superior service and selection! We look forward to seeing you!
      </div>
      <a class="welcome-link" href="/about-us-harley-davidson-dealership--info" title="About Adventure Harley-Davidson® in Dover, OH">
       Learn More About Us
      </a>

  <script>
   // Sticky Nav - Added [[Date]] by [[Agent]]
(function() {
    var nav = $('#main-nav'), // select navbar here
        stickyOffset = nav.offset().top,
        padding = nav.height();
 
    $(window).scroll(function() {
        var scroll = $(window).scrollTop();
        if (scroll >= stickyOffset) {
            nav.addClass('sticky-nav');
            $('html').css({ paddingTop: padding + "px"})
        } else {
            nav.removeClass('sticky-nav');
            $('html').removeAttr('style');
        }
    });
}());
  </script>

  <script>
   // location field hidden in css
	// auto-select the location of the site the vehicle is viewed on
	// NOT the location of the unit, or the user-provided location (hidden css)
	$(document).on('click','form',function(){
		var vehLocation = $(this).find('#formLocations select[name="location"]');
		if (vehLocation.length > 0 && vehLocation.val().length < 1) {
			$(vehLocation.find('option')[1]).attr('selected','true');
		}
	});
  </script>
